Generating .MTREE

CMD: bsdtar -czf .MTREE --format=mtree --options=!all,use-set,type,uid,mode,time,size,md5,sha256,link .PKGINFO usr var

Tar-ing up files

CMD: bsdtar -cf - .PKGINFO usr var .MTREE

CMD: xz -c -z

Successfully ran bsdtar -cf - .PKGINFO usr var .MTREE | xz -c -z

CMD: bsdtar -tqf ponysay.pkg.tar.xz .PKGINFO
# .PKGINFO

Created package at path /var/cache/pacman/pkg/ponysay.pkg.tar.xz
